        </span><p data-testid="dcac-cfe-overview"><span>Subscribe to advanced credit and debit card payment events using an event
            listener. Event listeners can help you update the UI of your form based on the state of the fields.</span></p><span>

                    <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Triggers when the payer requests submission of an input field. For example, when pressing Enter

            </span><h2 class="newH2 content-title ">1. Set up
                event listener</h2><span>
            </span><p><span>Set up an event listener using the advanced credit and debit card payments </span><code class=""><span>on()</span></code><span> function.
                Use the event object to get information about your fields and update your UI.</span></p><span>

            </span><h2 class="newH2 content-title ">2. Get the
                state of your form</h2><span>
            </span><p><span>Use the </span><code class=""><span>getState</span></code><span> function to get the state of your form without using events.</span></p><span>
            </span><h3>getState Example</h3><span>

        </span><div class="homepage-PPCP-marginTop60"><span>
            </span><h2 class="newH2 content-title ">Sample event
                listeners</h2><span>
            </span><p><span>The following examples show how to use event listeners.</span></p><span>
            </span><ul><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-focus" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>focus</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-blur" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>blur</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-empty" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>empty</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-notempty" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>notEmpty</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-cardtypechange" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>cardTypeChange</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-validitychange" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>validityChange</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-event-inputsubmitrequest" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>inputSubmitRequest</span></code></a><span>
                </span></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>
            </span><h4 id="link-event-focus" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-event-focus" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-event-focus" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->focus</h4><span>
            </span><p><span>This event triggers when a field gains focus.</span></p><span>
            </span><div class="new-codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div><span>
                        </span><span>
                    </span></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB"             </span><h4 id="link-event-validitychange" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-event-validitychange" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-event-validitychange" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->validityChange</h4><span>

                </span></div><span>
            </span></div><span>
            </span><h4 id="link-event-inputsubmitrequest" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-event-inputsubmitrequest" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-event-inputsubmitrequest" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->inputSubmitRequest</h4><span>
            </span><p><span>This event triggers when the payer requests submission of an input field. For example, when pressing
                </span><span class="boldText"><span>Enter</span></span><span> or </span><span class="boldText"><span>Return</span></span><span> on the keyboard.
            </span></p><span>

        </span><div><span>
            </span><h2 class="newH2 ">Methods</h2><span>
            </span><p><span>The following methods are supported on parent and individual card fields:</span></p><span>
            </span><ul><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-render" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>render()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-iseligible" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>isEligible()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-addclass" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>addClass()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-clear" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>clear()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-focus" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>focus()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-getstate" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>getstate()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-on" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>on()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-removeattribute" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>removeAttribute()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-setattribute" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>setAttribute()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-removeclass" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>removeClass()</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-method-setmessage" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>setMessage()</span></code></a></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>
            </span><h3 id="link-method-render" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-method-render" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-method-render" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->render()</h3><span>
            </span><div class="new-codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div><span>
                        </span><span>
                    </span></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">render</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token plain">options</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">{</span><span class="token known-class-name class-name" style="color:rgb(78, 201, 176)">Promise</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">|</span><span class="token keyword" style="color:rgb(86, 156, 214)">void</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">}</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
            </span></div><span>
            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>render()</span></code><span> method creates an instance of advanced credit and debit card payments and
                renders the card fields for checkout based on the mapping and styles provided by </span><code class=""><span>options</span></code><span>.
            </span></p><span>
            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>options</span></code><span> object maps the HTML element to each of the advanced credit and debit card
                payment inputs, style, and properties.</span></p><span>
            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>options</span></code><span> object contains the following fields:</span></p><span>
            </span><ul><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>createOrder</span></code><span>: A callback field that returns the </span><code class=""><span>order-id</span></code><span> value. The
                    </span><code class=""><span>order-id</span></code><span> is a required reference ID for each order created. The </span><code class=""><span>order-id</span></code><span>
                    also associates the payer's card details with the order created.
                </span></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>styles</span></code><span>: A </span><a href="#link-type-styleoptions" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>styleOptions</span></a><span>
                    parameter that defines the styling applied on each of the advanced credit and debit card payments
                    inputs.</span></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>fields</span></code><span>: A </span><a href="#link-type-fieldoptions" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>fieldOptions</span></a><span>
                    parameter that defines the mapping of the HTML element to the advanced credit and debit card
                    payments inputs and their properties.</span></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>
            </span><h3 id="link-method-iseligible" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-method-iseligible" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-method-iseligible" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->isEligible()</h3><span>
            </span><div class="new-codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div><span>
                        </span><span>
                    </span></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">isEligible</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">{</span><span class="token plain">boolean</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">}</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
            </span></div><span>
            </span><p><span> The </span><code class=""><span>isEligible()</span></code><span> method checks if advanced credit and debit card payments are eligible to
                render based on configuration and business rules.</span></p><span>
            </span><h3 id="link-method-addclass" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-method-addclass" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-method-addclass" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->addClass()</h3><span>
            </span><div class="new-codeBlocks-wrapper"><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div><span>
                        </span><span>
                    </span></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
                </span><div><span>
                    </span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">addClass</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token plain">field</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"> classname</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"> callback</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">&lt;</span><span class="token plain">sub</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">&gt;</span><span class="token plain">opt</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">&lt;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">/</span><span class="token plain">sub</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">{</span><span class="token known-class-name class-name" style="color:rgb(78, 201, 176)">Promise</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">|</span><span class="token keyword" style="color:rgb(86, 156, 214)">void</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">}</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
                </span></div><span>
            </span></div><span>
            </span><p><span> The </span><code class=""><span>addClass1()</span></code><span> method adds a class to a field. Use this method to update field styles when
                events occur elsewhere in your checkout integration. Includes the following parameters:</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">
                <thead class="css-t6o7m3-thead" data-ppui="true">
                    <tr class="css-usjykh-row_base-row_head" data-ppui="true">
                        <th><span>Parameter</span></th>
                        <th><span>Type</span></th>
                        <th><span>Description</span></th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody class="css-1da1jgi-tbody" data-ppui="true">
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>field</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">The field you want to add a class to. Must be a valid <code class=""><span>fieldOption</span></code>.</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">

                </span></div><span>
            </span></div><span>
            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>on()</span></code><span> method subscribes a handler function to a named event. Events include:</span></p><span>
            </span><ul><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>blur</span></code></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>focus</span></code></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>empty</span></code></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>notEmpty</span></code></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>cardTypeChange</span></code></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>validityChange</span></code></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>
            </span><p><span>Events trigger a </span><code class=""><span>stateObject</span></code><span>, which includes the following parameters:</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">The name of the event to which you are subscribing.</td>

            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>removeAttribute()</span></code><span> method removes a supported attribute from a field. Includes the
                following parameters:</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">
                <thead class="css-t6o7m3-thead" data-ppui="true">
                    <tr class="css-usjykh-row_base-row_head" data-ppui="true">
                        <th><span>Parameter</span></th>
                        <th><span>Type</span></th>
                        <th><span>Description</span></th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object</td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">The options for the attribute you want to remove: <br/> - <code class=""><span>field</span></code>: A string field
                            from which you want to remove an attribute. Must be a valid <code class=""><span>fieldOption</span></code>.<br/> -
                            <code class=""><span>attribute</span></code>: The name of the attribute you want to remove from the field.
                        </td>
                    </tr>

            </span></div><span>
            </span><p><span>The </span><code class=""><span>setMessage()</span></code><span> method sets a visually hidden message for screen readers on a field.</span></p><span>
            </span><p><span>Includes the following </span><code class=""><span>options</span></code><span> parameter, which contains the following:</span></p><span>
            </span><ul><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>field</span></code><span>: A string field from which you want to add an attribute. Must be a valid
                    </span><code class=""><span>fieldOption</span></code><span>.
                </span></li><span>
                </span><li><code class=""><span>message</span></code><span>: The message to set.</span></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>

        </span><div class="homepage-PPCP-marginTop60"><span>
            </span><h2 class="newH2 ">Type definitions</h2><span>
            </span><p><span>Card field events use the following types of information:</span></p><span>

                </span><li><a href="#link-type-cardsecuritycode" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>cardSecurityCode</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-type-hostedfieldscard" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>hostedFieldsCard</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>hostedFieldsFieldData</span></code></a></li><span>
                </span><li><a href="#link-type-stateobject" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><code class="linkCard"><span>stateObject</span></code></a></li><span>
            </span></ul><span>

                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_respdx-anchor css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><a aria-hidden="true" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent" href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#formatinputbooleanallow-or-deny-automatic-formatting-on-this-field.-default-is-true." pa-marked="1"></a><code class=""><span>formatInput</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">boolean</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>Allow or deny automatic formatting on this field. Default is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>true</span></code><span>.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_respdx-anchor css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><a aria-hidden="true" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent" href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#maskinputobject-or-booleanallow-or-deny-input-masking-when-input-is-not-focused.-if-set-to-true,-instead-of-an-object,-the-defaults-for-the-maskinput-parameters-are-used.-default-is-false.-the-object-properties-are:-character:-a-string-field-which-specifies-the-character-to-use-when-masking-the-input.-the-default-character-(&#x27;%E2%80%A2&#x27;)-uses-a-unicode-symbol,-so-the-web-page-must-support-utf-8-characters-when-using-the-default.-showlastfour:-a-boolean-field-applicable-only-for-the-credit-card-field.-defines-whether-to-show-the-last-4-digits-of-the-card-when-masking.-default-is-false." pa-marked="1"></a><code class=""><span>maskInput</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object or boolean</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>Allow or deny input masking when input is not focused. If set to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>true</span></code><span>, instead of an object, the defaults for the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>maskInput</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>parameters are used. Default is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>false</span></code><span>. The object properties are:</span><br style="box-sizing:inherit"/><code class=""><span>character</span></code><span>: A string field which specifies the character to use when masking the input. The default character ('') uses a Unicode symbol, so the web page must support UTF-8 characters when using the default.</span><br style="box-sizing:inherit"/><code class=""><span>showLastFour</span></code><span>: A Boolean field applicable only for the credit card field. Defines whether to show the last 4 digits of the card when masking. Default is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>false</span></code><span>.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_resp css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>maxCardLength</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>This option only applies to the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>number</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field. Limits the card number length, even if the card brand supports longer card numbers. If the value that is passed is greater than the max length for a card brand, the smaller of the two values is used. For example, if</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>maxCardLength</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is set to 16, but an American Express card, which has a max card length of 15, is entered, the max card length is 15.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_resp css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>maxlength</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>This option applies only to the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>cvv</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field. Used as the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>maxlength</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>attribute of the input if it is less than the default. The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>maxlength</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>option is most often used to limit the length of the CVV input for CVV-only verifications when the card type is known, and to limit the length of the postal code input when cards are coming from a known region.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_resp css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>minlength</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">number</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>This option applies only to the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>cvv</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field. Used as the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>minlength</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>attribute of the input. The default value is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>3</span></code><span>. The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>minlength</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>attribute applies only to integrations capturing a CVV without a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>number</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_resp css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>prefill</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">string</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>A value to be used to pre-fill the field. For example, when creating an update card form, you can pre-fill the expiration date fields with the old expiration date.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-1a18ksn-row_base-row_resp css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1tf2qhy-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_a12 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>rejectUnsupportedCards</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">boolean</td>
                        <td class="css-evg6bs-text_body-align_start-cell_resp-m_b3 css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><span style="box-sizing:inherit"><span>Allow only card types that your merchant account can process. Unsupported card types invalidate the card form. For example, if you only process Visa cards, a payer entering an American Express card would get an invalid card field. This can be used only for the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>number</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field. The default is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>false</span></code><span>.</span></span></td>
                    </tr>
                </tbody>
            </table><br/><span>
            </span><p></p><span>

            </span><h3 id="link-type-styleoptions" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-type-styleoptions" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-type-styleoptions" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->styleOptions</h3><span>
            </span><p><span>An object that represents CSS that is applied in each card field. This object looks similar to CSS, and
                changes font styles such as </span><code class=""><span>font-family</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>color</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
            </span><p><span>You can also pass the name of a class on your site that contains the styles you want to apply. The style
                properties are automatically pulled from the class and applied to the card field inputs
            </span></p><span>
            </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>.</span></p><span>
            </span><div style="box-sizing:inherit;display:flex;border:1pxsolidrgba(0,0,0,0.1);padding:24px;border-radius:12px;flex-direction:row;justify-content:flex-start;background-color:rgb(255,255,255)!important;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial" class="archetypeTip archetypeTip-warning"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0,0,48,48" width="48" fill="none" height="48"><span>
                    </span><path d="M42.6667,23.9999C42.6667,34.3092,34.3093,42.6666,24,42.6666C13.6907,42.6666,5.33334,34.3092,5.33334,23.9999C5.33334,13.6906,13.6907,5.33325,24,5.33325C34.3093,5.33325,42.6667,13.6906,42.6667,23.9999ZM22.5668,34.5833H25.4268C25.8168,34.5833,26.0248,34.3753,26.0248,33.9853V21.8479C26.0248,21.4579,25.8168,21.2499,25.4268,21.2499H22.5668C22.1768,21.2499,21.9688,21.4579,21.9688,21.8479V33.9853C21.9688,34.3753,22.1768,34.5833,22.5668,34.5833ZM24,17.3333C25.4728,17.3333,26.6667,16.1393,26.6667,14.6666C26.6667,13.1938,25.4728,11.9999,24,11.9999C22.5273,11.9999,21.3333,13.1938,21.3333,14.6666C21.3333,16.1393,22.5273,17.3333,24,17.3333Z" clip-rule="evenodd" fill="#003087" fill-rule="evenodd"></path><span>
                </span></svg><span>
                </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:9px0px0px6px" class="tipText"><span style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:700;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-right:0.5rem" class="boldText"><span>Note:</span></span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>Using</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>styleOptions</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is recommended only for input elements. </span><h3 id="cardsecuritycode" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#cardsecuritycode" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#cardsecuritycode" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->cardSecurityCode</h3><span>

            </span><p><span>Information about the security code for a card.</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">

                            <code class=""><span>Diners Club</span></code> <br/> <code class=""><span>Discover</span></code> <br/> <code class=""><span>JCB</span></code> <br/>

                            <code class=""><span>Visa</span></code>
                        </td>

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">object <a href="#link-type-cardsecuritycode" class="linkFormat dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>cardSecurityCode</span></a>
                        </td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Contains data about the card brand&#x27;s security code requirements. For example, on a Visa
                            card, the <code class=""><span>CVV</span></code> is 3 digits, while on an American Express card, the
                            <code class=""><span>CID</span></code> is 4 digits.
                        </td>

            </span><h3 id="link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->hostedFieldsFieldData</h3><span>
            </span><p><span>Fields data for advanced credit and debit card payments is sent in </span><code class=""><span>stateObjects</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">
                <thead class="css-t6o7m3-thead" data-ppui="true">
                    <tr class="css-usjykh-row_base-row_head" data-ppui="true">
                        <th><span>Property</span></th>
                        <th><span>Type</span></th>
                        <th><span>Description</span></th>
                    </tr>
                </thead>
                <tbody class="css-1da1jgi-tbody" data-ppui="true">
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>container</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">HTML element</td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">The container DOM element on your page associated with the current event.</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>isFocused</span></code></td>

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Whether the input is currently focused.</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>isEmpty</span></code></td>

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Whether the user has entered a value in the input.</td>
                    </tr>
                    <tr class="css-13cxzri-row_base" data-ppui="true">
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true"><code class=""><span>isPotentiallyValid</span></code></td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">boolean</td>
                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Whether the current input could potentially be valid. For example, if a payer is entering a
                            card number and types &quot;41&quot;, the field recognizes that the input can become a valid entry.
                            However, if the payer enters &quot;4x&quot; it is clear that the card number can&#x27;t become valid. The
                            value is true if the entry can become valid, and false if it can&#x27;t.</td>
                    </tr>

                        <td class="css-1d2f8tx-text_body-align_start" data-ppui="true">Whether the input is valid and can be submitted.</td>

            </span><h3 id="link-type-stateobject" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#link-type-stateobject" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#link-type-stateobject" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->stateObject</h3><span>
            </span><p><span>The event payload is sent from </span><code class=""><span>on</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>getState</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
            </span><table data-ppui-info="table_3.22.1__7.46.3" class="ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm ppvx_table ppvx_table-responsive-sm css-16a5cik-text_body-legacy_table-text_body_strong-align_start-w100">

                            <code class=""><span>credit-card-type</span></code>, an open-source card detection library.
                        </td>

If you are integrated with the CardFields component, see [Card\n            Field Events](/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields-events/) .\n\nSubscribe to advanced credit and debit card payment events using an event\n            listener. Event listeners can help you update the UI of your form based on the state of the fields.\n\nYou can subscribe to the following events:\n\n| Event name | Description |\n| --- | --- |\n| [focus](#link-event-focus) | Triggers when a field gains focus. |\n| [blur](#link-event-blur) | Triggers when a field loses focus. |\n| [empty](#link-event-empty) | Triggers when a field transitions from having data to being empty. |\n| [notEmpty](#link-event-notempty) | Triggers when a field transitions from being empty to having data. |\n| [cardTypeChange](#link-event-cardtypechange) | Triggers when the possible card type changes. Only triggered by a change in the number field. |\n| [validityChange](#link-event-validitychange) | Triggers when the validity of a field changes. |\n| [inputSubmitRequest](#link-event-inputsubmitrequest) | Triggers when the payer requests submission of an input field. For example, when pressing Enter\n                        or Return on the keyboard. |\n\n## 1. Set up\n                event listener\nSet up an event listener using the advanced credit and debit card payments on() function.\n                Use the event object to get information about your fields and update your UI.\n\n\u0026lt;ContentAccordion\u0026gt;\n    \u0026lt;AccordionRow heading=\"cardTypeChange Example\"\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;p\n        style=\"margin-top: 3rem;\"\n        data-testid=\"dcac-cfe-acc1-p0\"\n      \u0026gt;\n        Here is an example of how to use \u0026lt;code\u0026gt;cardTypeChange\u0026lt;/code\u0026gt; to update your CVV label and placeholder:\n      \u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;NewCodeBlockWrapper\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;NewCodeBlock\n          className=\"language-javascript\"\n          children={`\n            paypal.HostedFields.render({ /* ... */ }).then(function (hostedFieldsInstance) {\n              var cvvLabel = document.querySelector('label[for=\"cvv\"]'); // The label for your CVV field\n            \n              hostedFieldsInstance.on('cardTypeChange', function (event) {\n                // This event triggers when a change in card type is detected.\n                // It triggers only from the number field.\n                var cvvText;\n            \n                if (event.cards.length === 1) {\n                  cvvText = event.cards[0].code.name;\n                } else {\n                  cvvText = 'CVV';\n                }\n            \n                cvvLabel.innerHTML = cvvText;\n            \n                hostedFieldsInstance.setAttribute({\n                  field: 'cvv',\n                  attribute: 'placeholder',\n                  value: cvvText\n                });\n              });\n            });\n          `}\n        /\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;/NewCodeBlockWrapper\u0026gt;\n    \u0026lt;/AccordionRow\u0026gt;\n  \u0026lt;/ContentAccordion\u0026gt;## 2. Get the\n                state of your form\nUse the getState function to get the state of your form without using events.\n\n### getState Example\nThe following example uses getState to confirm that all provided fields are valid before form submission:\n\n1varform=document.querySelector('#my-sample-form');23paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){4form.addEventListener('submit',function(event){5varstate=hostedFieldsInstance.getState();6varformValid=Object.keys(state.fields).every(function(key){7returnstate.fields[key].isValid;8});910if(formValid){11// Submit hosted fields card data12hostedFieldsInstance.submit();13}else{14// Let the payer know their fields are invalid15}16});17});## Sample event\n                listeners\nThe following examples show how to use event listeners.\n\n- [focus](#link-event-focus)\n- [blur](#link-event-blur)\n- [empty](#link-event-empty)\n- [notEmpty](#link-event-notempty)\n- [cardTypeChange](#link-event-cardtypechange)\n- [validityChange](#link-event-validitychange)\n- [inputSubmitRequest](#link-event-inputsubmitrequest) \n\n#### focus\nThis event triggers when a field gains focus.\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('focus',function(event){3// Your actions on focus4console.log(event.emittedBy,'gained focus');5});6});#### blur\nThis event triggers when a field loses focus.\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('blur',function(event){3// Your actions on blur4console.log(event.emittedBy,'lost focus');5});6});#### empty\nThis event triggers when a field transitions from having data to being empty.\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('empty',function(event){3// Your actions on empty4console.log(event.emittedBy,'is now empty');5});6});#### notEmpty\nThis event triggers when a field transitions from being empty to having data.\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('notEmpty',function(event){3console.log(event.emittedBy,'has data');4});5});#### cardTypeChange\nThis event triggers when activity within the number field has changed, so the possible card type has also\n                changed.\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('cardTypeChange',function(event){3if(event.cards.length===1){4console.log(event.cards[0].type);5}else{6console.log('Type of card not yet known');7}8});9});#### validityChange\nThis event triggers when the validity of a field has changed. Validity is represented in the event object\n                as two booleans: isValid and isPotentiallyValid .\n\n1paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){2hostedFieldsInstance.on('validityChange',function(event){3varfield=event.fields[event.emittedBy];45if(field.isValid){6console.log(event.emittedBy,'is fully valid');7}elseif(field.isPotentiallyValid){8console.log(event.emittedBy,'is potentially valid');9}else{10console.log(event.emittedBy,'is not valid');11}12});13});#### inputSubmitRequest\nThis event triggers when the payer requests submission of an input field. For example, when pressing Enter or Return on the keyboard.\n\n1varhostedFields=require('braintree-web/hosted-fields');2varsubmitButton=document.querySelector('input[type=\"submit\"]');34paypal.HostedFields.render({/* ... */}).then(function(hostedFieldsInstance){5hostedFieldsInstance.on('inputSubmitRequest',function(){6// User requested submission, e.g. by pressing Enter or equivalent7submitButton.click();8});9});## Methods\nThe following methods are supported on parent and individual card fields:\n\n- [render()](#link-method-render)\n- [isEligible()](#link-method-iseligible)\n- [addClass()](#link-method-addclass)\n- [clear()](#link-method-clear)\n- [focus()](#link-method-focus)\n- [getstate()](#link-method-getstate)\n- [on()](#link-method-on)\n- [removeAttribute()](#link-method-removeattribute)\n- [setAttribute()](#link-method-setattribute)\n- [removeClass()](#link-method-removeclass)\n- [setMessage()](#link-method-setmessage)\n\n### render()\n1render(options){Promise|void}The render() method creates an instance of advanced credit and debit card payments and\n                renders the card fields for checkout based on the mapping and styles provided by options .\n\nThe options object maps the HTML element to each of the advanced credit and debit card\n                payment inputs, style, and properties.\n\nThe options object contains the following fields:\n\n- createOrder : A callback field that returns the order-id value. The order-id is a required reference ID for each order created. The order-id also associates the payer's card details with the order created.\n- styles : A [styleOptions](#link-type-styleoptions) parameter that defines the styling applied on each of the advanced credit and debit card payments\n                    inputs.\n- fields : A [fieldOptions](#link-type-fieldoptions) parameter that defines the mapping of the HTML element to the advanced credit and debit card\n                    payments inputs and their properties.\n\n### isEligible()\n1isEligible(){boolean}The isEligible() method checks if advanced credit and debit card payments are eligible to\n                render based on configuration and business rules.\n\n### addClass()\n1addClass(field,classname,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){Promise|void}The addClass1() method adds a class to a field. Use this method to update field styles when\n                events occur elsewhere in your checkout integration. Includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| field | string | The field you want to add a class to. Must be a validfieldOption. |\n| classname | string | The class to be added. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### clear()\n1clear(field,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){Promise|void}The clear() method clears the value of a field. Includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| field | string | The field you want to clear. Must be a validfieldOption. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### focus()\n1focus(field,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){void}The focus() method places focus on a field. Includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| field | string | The field you want to focus. Must be a validfieldOption. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### getState()\n1getState(){object}The getState() method returns an object that includes the state of all fields\n                and possible card types.\n\n### on()\n1on(event,handler){void}The on() method subscribes a handler function to a named event. Events include:\n\n- blur\n- focus\n- empty\n- notEmpty\n- cardTypeChange\n- validityChange\n\nEvents trigger a stateObject , which includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| event | string | The name of the event to which you are subscribing. |\n| handler | callback | A callback to handle the event. |\n\n### removeAttribute()\n1removeAttribute(options,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){Promise|void}The removeAttribute() method removes a supported attribute from a field. Includes the\n                following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| options | object | The options for the attribute you want to remove: -field: A string field\n                            from which you want to remove an attribute. Must be a validfieldOption. -attribute: The name of the attribute you want to remove from the field. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### setAttribute()\n1setAttribute(options,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){Promise|void}The setAttribute() method sets an attribute of a field. Supported attributes are aria-invalid , aria-required , disabled , and placeholder . Includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| options | object | The options for the attribute you want to set. -field: A string field from\n                            which you want to add an attribute. Must be a validfieldOption. -attribute: The name of the attribute you want to add to the field. -value: The value for the attribute. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### removeClass()\n1removeClass(field,classname,callback\u0026lt;sub\u0026gt;opt\u0026lt;/sub\u0026gt;){Promise|void}The removeClass() method removes a class from a field. Use this class to update field styles\n                when events occur elsewhere in your checkout integration. Includes the following parameters:\n\n| Parameter | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| field | string | The field you want to remove a class from. Must be a validfieldOption. |\n| classname | string | The class you want to remove. |\n| callback | callback | This callback triggers on completion. It passes any errors that occur during the call. This\n                            returns no data if the call successfully adds the class. |\n\n### setMessage()\n1setMessage(options){void}The setMessage() method sets a visually hidden message for screen readers on a field.\n\nIncludes the following options parameter, which contains the following:\n\n- field : A string field from which you want to add an attribute. Must be a valid fieldOption .\n- message : The message to set.\n\n## Type definitions\nCard field events use the following types of information:\n\n- [field](#link-type-field)\n- [fieldOptions](#link-type-fieldoptions)\n- [styleOptions](#link-type-styleoptions)\n- [cardSecurityCode](#link-type-cardsecuritycode)\n- [hostedFieldsCard](#link-type-hostedfieldscard)\n- [hostedFieldsFieldData](#link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata)\n- [stateObject](#link-type-stateobject)\n\n### field\nFields used in [fieldOptions](#link-type-fieldoptions) object.\n\n\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#selectorstringa-css-selector-to-find-the-container-where-the-card-fields-are-inserted.)selector | string | A CSS selector to find the container where the card fields are inserted. |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#placeholderstringused-as-the-placeholder-attribute-of-the-input.-if-the-browser-doesn't-natively-supportplaceholder,-it-is-polyfilled.)placeholder | string | Used as theplaceholderattribute of the input. If the browser doesn't natively supportplaceholder, it is polyfilled. |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#typestringthe-type-attribute-of-the-input.-for-example,-to-mask-cvv-input-use-type:-%22password%22.)type | string | Thetypeattribute of the input. For example, to maskCVVinput usetype: \"password\". |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#formatinputbooleanallow-or-deny-automatic-formatting-on-this-field.-default-is-true.)formatInput | boolean | Allow or deny automatic formatting on this field. Default istrue. |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/card-fields/v1/events/#maskinputobject-or-booleanallow-or-deny-input-masking-when-input-is-not-focused.-if-set-to-true,-instead-of-an-object,-the-defaults-for-the-maskinput-parameters-are-used.-default-is-false.-the-object-properties-are:-character:-a-string-field-which-specifies-the-character-to-use-when-masking-the-input.-the-default-character-('%E2%80%A2')-uses-a-unicode-symbol,-so-the-web-page-must-support-utf-8-characters-when-using-the-default.-showlastfour:-a-boolean-field-applicable-only-for-the-credit-card-field.-defines-whether-to-show-the-last-4-digits-of-the-card-when-masking.-default-is-false.)maskInput | object or boolean | Allow or deny input masking when input is not focused. If set totrue, instead of an object, the defaults for themaskInputparameters are used. Default isfalse. The object properties are: character: A string field which specifies the character to use when masking the input. The default character ('') uses a Unicode symbol, so the web page must support UTF-8 characters when using the default. showLastFour: A Boolean field applicable only for the credit card field. Defines whether to show the last 4 digits of the card when masking. Default isfalse. |\n| maxCardLength | number | This option only applies to thenumberfield. Limits the card number length, even if the card brand supports longer card numbers. If the value that is passed is greater than the max length for a card brand, the smaller of the two values is used. For example, ifmaxCardLengthis set to 16, but an American Express card, which has a max card length of 15, is entered, the max card length is 15. |\n| maxlength | number | This option applies only to thecvvfield. Used as themaxlengthattribute of the input if it is less than the default. Themaxlengthoption is most often used to limit the length of the CVV input for CVV-only verifications when the card type is known, and to limit the length of the postal code input when cards are coming from a known region. |\n| minlength | number | This option applies only to thecvvfield. Used as theminlengthattribute of the input. The default value is3. Theminlengthattribute applies only to integrations capturing a CVV without anumberfield. |\n| prefill | string | A value to be used to pre-fill the field. For example, when creating an update card form, you can pre-fill the expiration date fields with the old expiration date. |\n| rejectUnsupportedCards | boolean | Allow only card types that your merchant account can process. Unsupported card types invalidate the card form. For example, if you only process Visa cards, a payer entering an American Express card would get an invalid card field. This can be used only for thenumberfield. The default isfalse. |\n\n \n\n### fieldOptions\nAn object that has [field](#link-type-field) objects for each field.\n                Used in [render](#link-method-render) method.\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| number | object[field](#link-type-field) | A field for card number. |\n| expirationDate | object[field](#link-type-field) | A field for expiration date inMM/YYYYorMM/YYformat. |\n| cvv | object[field](#link-type-field) | A field for a 3 or 4 digit card verification code, such asCVVorCID. |\n\n### styleOptions\nAn object that represents CSS that is applied in each card field. This object looks similar to CSS, and\n                changes font styles such as font-family or color .\n\nYou can also pass the name of a class on your site that contains the styles you want to apply. The style\n                properties are automatically pulled from the class and applied to the card field inputs\n\n.\n\nNote:  Using  styleOptions  is recommended only for input elements. If you use a  select  style for the expiration date, unexpected styling might occur.\n\n### cardSecurityCode\nInformation about the security code for a card.\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| name | string | The name of security code for card. Valid values areCVV,CID, andCVC. |\n| size | number | The expected length of the security code, which is most often3or4. |\n\n### hostedFieldsCard\nInformation about the card type, sent in stateObjects .\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| type | string | The code-friendly card type. Valid values are: american-express diners-club discover jcb maestro master-card unionpay visa |\n| niceType | string | The human-readable card type. Valid values: American Express Diners Club Discover JCB Maestro MasterCard UnionPay Visa |\n| code | object[cardSecurityCode](#link-type-cardsecuritycode) | Contains data about the card brand's security code requirements. For example, on a Visa\n                            card, theCVVis 3 digits, while on an American Express card, theCIDis 4 digits. |\n\n### hostedFieldsFieldData\nFields data for advanced credit and debit card payments is sent in stateObjects .\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| container | HTML element | The container DOM element on your page associated with the current event. |\n| isFocused | boolean | Whether the input is currently focused. |\n| isEmpty | boolean | Whether the user has entered a value in the input. |\n| isPotentiallyValid | boolean | Whether the current input could potentially be valid. For example, if a payer is entering a\n                            card number and types \"41\", the field recognizes that the input can become a valid entry.\n                            However, if the payer enters \"4x\" it is clear that the card number can't become valid. The\n                            value is true if the entry can become valid, and false if it can't. |\n| isValid | boolean | Whether the input is valid and can be submitted. |\n\n### stateObject\nThe event payload is sent from on or getState .\n\n| Property | Type | Description |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| cards | array | Returns an array of potential cards. If the card type has been determined, the array\n                            contains only one card. Advanced credit and debit card payments usecredit-card-type, an open-source card detection library. |\n| emittedBy | string | The name of the field associated with an event. This is not included if returned bygetState. Valid values are\"number\",\"cvv\", and\"expirationDate\". |\n| fields | object[hostedFieldsFieldData](#link-type-hostedfieldsfielddata) | Contains data about the field in the context of the event. Valid values are\"number\",\"cvv\", and\"expirationDate\". |\n\n"},"routes/__docs-pages":null},"actionData":null,"errors":null},"future":{"v2_dev":true,"unstable_postcss":false,"unstable_tailwind":false,"v2_errorBoundary":false,"v2_headers":false,"v2_meta":true,"v2_normalizeFormMethod":true,"v2_routeConvention":false}};</script><script nonce="DN8QAJ7bHTuzdKT5ciuw3HfnqsOC40gsYp9pSj3PA63tIpQu" type="module" async="">import "https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/bundles/10.6.8/manifest-2AA28ED2.js";

if (cookieBannerUi && cookieBannerUi.className.indexOf('ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile') === -1) { cookieBannerUi.className += " ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile"; } }; window.showGdprBanner = function () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if (cookieBannerUi) { cookieBannerUi.className = cookieBannerUi.className.replace("ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile",""); } }; document.body.addEventListener("focus", function (event) { if (event.target.type === 'text' || event.target.type === 'number' || event.target.type === 'password' || event.target.type === 'email' || event.target.type === 'select-one') { window.hideGdprBanner(); } }, true); } function adjustPaddingTop(){ var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && bannerHeight){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingTop = bannerHeight/16 +'em'; } } }; var isPaddingBottomAdded = false, bannerPaddingBottom = ""; function adjustPaddingBottom(addListener){ if (undefined || !false) { return; } function adjustPaddingBottomEvent() { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var bodyPaddingBottom = cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom; var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none') { if (bodyPaddingBottom === "" || (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom === bodyPaddingBottom)) { var cookieBannerContainer = document.getElementsByClassName('ccpaCookieBanner_container'); var bannerBottomHeight = cookieBannerContainer.length > 0 ? parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(cookieBannerContainer[0]).bottom.replace("px", "")) : 0; var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; bannerPaddingBottom = ((bannerHeight + bannerBottomHeight) / 16) + 'em'; cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom = bannerPaddingBottom; isPaddingBottomAdded = true; } else if (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom !== bodyPaddingBottom) { isPaddingBottomAdded = false; } } } } if (addListener) { adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent);  } else { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent); adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); if (isPaddingBottomAdded && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom === bannerPaddingBottom) { cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-bottom'); } } } }; window.bindGdprEvents = bindGdprEvents; function cookieDisabled() { if (navigator.cookieEnabled === false) return "true"; else if (navigator.cookieEnabled === true) return "false"; else return "undefined"; }; function fptiLogActivity(winFptiData){ window.PAYPAL.analytics.Analytics.prototype.logActivity({...winFptiData, product:"cookieBanner"}); }; function gdprSetup () { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var manageLink = document.getElementById('manageCookiesLink'); var acceptAllLink = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var trackingPageName = '' || getFptiPage() || document.title; if(!isBannerClosed()){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled";    } } var pageName = trackingPageName || getFptiPage() || document.title; var winFptiData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((window && window.fpti) || {})); if(false){ bannerFptiData.isNativeBannerHidden = true; } for(var key in bannerFptiData){ winFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; winFptiData['event_name'] = 'cookie_banner_shown'; fptiLogActivity(winFptiData); if (manageLink) { manageLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|managecookies')); } if (acceptAllLink) { acceptAllLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|acceptcookies')); } bindGdprEvents(); }; function hideBanner() { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieLanguage && cookieBanner){ cookieLanguage.style.display = 'none'; cookieBanner.style.display = 'none'; }else { return false; } window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop); var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-top'); } document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll",""); document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("top-cookie-banner-enabled",""); return true; } function isPageReady () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); return !!(cookieBannerUi && getFptiReqData()); } function enableFocusEvent(addListener){ if(!false || undefined){ return; } var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); function focusIn(e) { if(cookieBanner && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none'){ var activeElement = document.activeElement; if(((activeElement.getBoundingClientRect().bottom) > (cookieBanner.getBoundingClientRect().top)) && !activeElement.parentElement.nodeName.includes("UL")){ activeElement.scrollIntoView({block: 'center'}); } }else{ document.removeEventListener("focusin", focusIn); } } if(addListener){ document.addEventListener("focusin",focusIn); } } function enableEvents(enable){ adjustPaddingBottom(enable); enableFocusEvent(enable); } var maxRetries = 34, bannerhidden=false; function triggerBanner() { if (isPageReady()) { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } gdprSetup(); } else { if (isBannerClosed() && !bannerhidden ) { bannerhidden=hideBanner(); } if (maxRetries-- > 0) { setTimeout(triggerBanner, 150); } else { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(!isBannerClosed() && document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner') && !document.body.className.includes("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll")){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled"; } } var acceptAllButton = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var bannerDeclineButton = document.getElementById('bannerDeclineButton'); var bannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('bannerCloseButton'); var usBannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('usBannerCloseButton'); }; } if ( bannerDeclineButton ) { bannerDeclineButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('decline')); }; } if ( usBannerCloseButton ) { usBannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); } } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } } } } triggerBanner(); })();</script></div></body></html>
